<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Spacing</h2><a id="user-content-spacing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Spacing" href="https://github.com/codewithsadee/grilli/blob/master/style-guide.md#spacing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-css notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-c1">--section-space</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">70<span class="pl-smi">px</span></span>;</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
